### [30] [Route-and-Reason: Scaling Large Language Model Reasoning with Reinforced Model Router](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.05901)
*Chenyang Shao,Xinyang Liu,Yutang Lin,Fengli Xu,Yong Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了解决大型语言模型（LLM）在进行复杂推理时计算成本高的问题，研究者们提出了一种名为R2-Reasoner的新框架。该框架利用一个基于强化学习的模型路由器，将复杂查询分解为子任务，并为每个子任务分配最合适的模型进行处理。这种细粒度的协作方式显著降低了成本，同时保持了推理的准确性。实验表明，R2-Reasoner相比现有技术，API成本降低了84.46%，并且在多个推理基准测试中表现出竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）的链式思考（Chain-of-thought）能力虽能提升复杂推理，但计算成本高昂。现有模型路由方法多在任务层面分配查询，未能实现模型间在更细粒度的子任务层面进行协作。这种细粒度的协作有望提高效率，但对路由器的调度、任务分解的质量和路由器的精度提出了巨大挑战。

Method: R2-Reasoner框架的核心是一个强化学习模型路由器。该路由器首先通过一个“分解器”将复杂查询拆解成子任务，然后由“子任务分配器”为每个子任务选择最优模型进行处理，从而在性能和成本之间取得平衡。路由器的训练采用两阶段交替进行的方式，结合了监督微调和强化学习，以实现有效的自我监督优化。实验在六个具有挑战性的推理基准上进行，对比了R2-Reasoner与现有先进基线方法的性能。

Result: 在六个具有挑战性的推理基准测试中，R2-Reasoner框架实现了显著的成本节约和竞争力的推理准确性。具体而言，与最先进的基线方法相比，该框架将API成本降低了84.46%，同时保持了相当的推理能力。

Conclusion: R2-Reasoner框架通过引入基于强化学习的细粒度模型路由和协作机制，有效地解决了LLM复杂推理中的成本与效率问题。该框架能够将复杂查询分解为子任务，并为每个子任务智能分配异构模型，从而在保证推理精度的前提下大幅降低了计算成本。这为构建更具可扩展性和效率的LLM推理系统铺平了道路。研究代码已开源。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought has been proven essential for enhancing the complex reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), but it also leads to high computational costs. Recent advances have explored the method to route queries among multiple models and proved it as a promising approach. However, previous works directly operate at the task level, i.e., assigning user queries to suitable LLMs, which does not allow hybrid LLMs to truly collaborate on finer-grained sub-tasks. Collaboration at the level of intermediate reasoning steps (thoughts) could enable more efficient coordination, but it also poses significant challenges for router scheduling, placing immense demands on the quality of task decomposition and the precision of the router. To address this, we propose R2-Reasoner, a novel framework centered around a Reinforced Model Router designed to efficiently scale LLM reasoning. This router orchestrates collaboration across nine heterogeneous models, whose parameter scales range from less than 1B to hundreds of billions, by first breaking down a complex query into subtasks with a decomposer, and then assigning each subtask to the optimal model with a subtask allocator, balancing performance with cost. Training this router involves a two-stage alternating process for the decomposer and the allocator, integrating supervised fine-tuning with reinforcement learning to enable effective self-supervised refinement. Extensive experiments across six challenging reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that R2-Reasoner reduces API costs by 84.46% compared with state-of-the-art baselines while maintaining competitive reasoning accuracy. Our framework paves the way for the development of more scalable and efficient reasoning systems. Our code is open-source at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/R2_Reasoner.

</details>


### [31] [QA-LIGN: Aligning LLMs through Constitutionally Decomposed QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.08123)
*Jacob Dineen,Aswin RRV,Qin Liu,Zhikun Xu,Xiao Ye,Ming Shen,Zhaonan Li,Shijie Lu,Chitta Baral,Muhao Chen,Ben Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为QA-LIGN的新方法，用于改进大型语言模型（LLMs）在遵循“有用、诚实、无害”等原则方面的对齐。QA-LIGN将单一的标量奖励分解为基于结构化自然语言程序的、可解释的、特定原则的评估。通过“草稿-批评-修订”的训练流程，模型可以获得透明的、针对不同原则的反馈，从而优化其响应。实验结果表明，QA-LIGN在减少模型受到攻击的成功率方面效果显著（最高可达68.7%），同时保持了极低的虚假拒绝率（0.67%），并在安全性和有用性之间取得了帕累托最优的性能。与现有的DPO和GRPO方法相比，QA-LIGN在同等训练资源下表现更优。研究强调了可解释和模块化的奖励信号能够提升LLM对齐的有效性和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在对齐“有用、诚实、无害”等原则时，通常依赖于单一的标量奖励。这种单一奖励模糊了驱动训练信号的具体目标，使得难以理解和改进模型行为。本研究旨在解决这一问题，通过提供更透明、可解释的奖励信号，以提升LLMs的对齐效果和安全性。

Method: 本研究提出QA-LIGN方法，将单一奖励分解为可解释的、基于结构化自然语言程序的、特定原则的评估。模型采用“草稿-批评-修订”的训练流程，在GRPO（Generalized Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback）框架下进行训练。在此流程中，针对模型响应的符号化评估（基于预设的评估标准）提供了透明的反馈，不仅包括初始响应，也包括修订后的响应。该方法应用于未经过滤的Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct模型。

Result: QA-LIGN方法在未经过滤的Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct模型上进行了评估。实验结果显示，QA-LIGN能够将攻击成功率降低高达68.7%，同时保持0.67%的低虚假拒绝率。在安全性和有用性之间，QA-LIGN实现了帕累托最优的性能。与标准的DPO（Direct Preference Optimization）和GRPO方法相比，QA-LIGN在同等训练条件下表现更优，甚至超越了使用最先进奖励模型的同等训练。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，使奖励信号可解释和模块化能够有效提升LLMs的对齐效果。QA-LIGN通过将奖励分解为可解释的、特定原则的评估，并结合“草稿-批评-修订”的训练流程，显著提高了模型的安全性（降低攻击成功率）和有用性，同时保持了较低的虚假拒绝率。研究结果强调了透明度在增强LLM安全性方面的重要性，并为未来开发更安全、更可信赖的LLMs提供了新的方向。研究的局限性可能在于评估标准的构建和泛化能力，未来的工作可以探索更自动化的评估标准生成以及在更多模型和任务上的应用。

Abstract: Alignment of large language models (LLMs) with principles like helpfulness, honesty, and harmlessness typically relies on scalar rewards that obscure which objectives drive the training signal. We introduce QA-LIGN, which decomposes monolithic rewards into interpretable principle-specific evaluations through structured natural language programs. Models learn through a draft, critique, and revise pipeline, where symbolic evaluation against the rubrics provides transparent feedback for both initial and revised responses during GRPO training. Applied to uncensored Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, QA-LIGN reduces attack success rates by up to 68.7% while maintaining a 0.67% false refusal rate, achieving Pareto optimal safety-helpfulness performance and outperforming both DPO and GRPO with state-of-the-art reward models given equivalent training. These results demonstrate that making reward signals interpretable and modular improves alignment effectiveness, suggesting transparency enhances LLM safety.

</details>


### [32] [Bridging Online Behavior and Clinical Insight: A Longitudinal LLM-based Study of Suicidality on YouTube Reveals Novel Digital Markers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.09495)
*Ilanit Sobol,Shir Lissak,Refael Tikochinski,Tal Nakash,Anat Brunstein Klomek,Eyal Fruchter,Roi Reichart*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究调查了YouTube用户自杀行为的语言模式，发现“心理健康困境”和“YouTube参与度”等话题与自杀企图相关，并与专家知识进行了比较。研究还发现，有既往自杀企图者倾向于帮助他人，而在此次企图期间仍活跃于YouTube者则更侧重于个人恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鉴于社交媒体日益普及，本研究旨在利用YouTube用户的数字足迹来理解自杀行为的语言模式，并探究这些模式与专家知识的异同，以期弥合数字行为与临床见解之间的差距。

Method: 研究分析了181个自杀企图者频道和134个对照组的纵向数据集。采用了三种分析方法：1. “自下而上”方法：使用大型语言模型（LLM）进行主题建模，识别与自杀企图相关的话题。2. “混合”方法：由临床专家审查LLM识别出的话题。3. “自上而下”方法：对自杀叙述进行心理学评估，分析个体动机。

Result: “自下而上”分析发现了166个话题，其中5个与自杀企图相关，“心理健康困境”和“YouTube参与度”这两个话题与自杀企图有显著关联（p < .01）。“混合”方法中，专家审查的话题未显示出比“自下而上”方法更显著的效果。心理学评估显示，有既往企图者分享经验旨在帮助他人（p<.01），而在此次企图期间仍活跃于YouTube者则更强调个人恢复（p<.01）。

Conclusion: 本研究通过结合“自下而上”、“混合”和“自上而下”的分析方法，为理解自杀行为提供了更细致的视角，并成功地将数字行为与临床见解联系起来。研究结果强调了“自下而上”方法在发现新见解方面的价值，并指出了不同自杀企图群体动机的差异。未来的研究可以进一步探索这些发现，并开发更有效的干预措施。

Abstract: Suicide remains a leading cause of death in Western countries. As social media becomes central to daily life, digital footprints offer valuable insight into suicidal behavior. Focusing on individuals who attempted suicide while uploading videos to their channels, we investigate: How do linguistic patterns on YouTube reflect suicidal behavior, and how do these patterns align with or differ from expert knowledge? We examined linguistic changes around suicide attempts and compared individuals who attempted suicide while actively uploading to their channel with three control groups: those with prior attempts, those experiencing major life events, and matched individuals from the broader cohort. Applying complementary bottom-up, hybrid, and expert-driven approaches, we analyzed a novel longitudinal dataset of 181 suicide-attempt channels and 134 controls. In the bottom-up analysis, LLM-based topic-modeling identified 166 topics; five were linked to suicide attempts, two also showed attempt-related temporal changes (Mental Health Struggles, $OR = 1.74$; YouTube Engagement, $OR = 1.67$; $p < .01$). In the hybrid approach, clinical experts reviewed LLM-derived topics and flagged 19 as suicide-related. However, none showed significant effects beyond those identified bottom-up. YouTube Engagement, a platform-specific indicator, was not flagged, underscoring the value of bottom-up discovery. A top-down psychological assessment of suicide narratives revealed differing motivations: individuals describing prior attempts aimed to help others ($β=-1.69$, $p<.01$), whereas those attempted during the uploading period emphasized personal recovery ($β=1.08$, $p<.01$). By integrating these approaches, we offer a nuanced understanding of suicidality, bridging digital behavior and clinical insights.

</details>


### [33] [An Investigation of Robustness of LLMs in Mathematical Reasoning: Benchmarking with Mathematically-Equivalent Transformation of Advanced Mathematical Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.08833)
*Yuren Hao,Xiang Wan,ChengXiang Zhai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种新的框架和数据集 (PutnamGAP) 来评估大型语言模型 (LLM) 在数学推理方面的鲁棒性，发现现有模型在面对语言和参数变化时性能会显著下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型在数学推理能力方面取得了显著进展，但对其鲁棒性的评估不足，尤其是在面对非数学扰动（如语言和参数变化）时，其性能稳定性有待考察。这项研究旨在通过系统性的压力测试来填补这一评估空白，以更准确地衡量 LLM 的真实数学推理能力，并为进一步改进模型提供指导。

Method: 研究提出了一种系统性框架，通过生成数学上等价但具有语言和参数变化的变体问题来对 LLM 进行压力测试。基于此框架，创建了一个名为 PutnamGAP 的新数据集，其中包含竞赛级数学问题的多种变体。然后，使用 PutnamGAP 数据集评估了多个系列的代表性 LLM，并分析了它们的鲁棒性。

Result: 在对 18 个商业和开源模型进行评估后，发现在面对 PutnamGAP 数据集中的变体问题时，所有模型的性能均出现显著下降。具体来说，OpenAI 的 O3 模型在原始问题上得分 51.5%，但在表面重命名变体上的得分下降了 4.7 个百分点，在参数化变体上的得分下降了 12.9 个百分点。相比之下，规模较小的模型表现更差。

Conclusion: 研究表明，所提出的评估方法能够有效加深对 LLM 数学推理鲁棒性的理解，并揭示了当前模型在该方面的不足。这些发现为未来改进 LLM 的数学推理能力提供了新的见解和方向。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce a systematic framework beyond conventional method to assess LLMs' mathematical-reasoning robustness by stress-testing them on advanced math problems that are mathematically equivalent but with linguistic and parametric variation. These transformations allow us to measure the sensitivity of LLMs to non-mathematical perturbations, thereby enabling a more accurate evaluation of their mathematical reasoning capabilities. Using this new evaluation methodology, we created PutnamGAP, a new benchmark dataset with multiple mathematically-equivalent variations of competition-level math problems. With the new dataset, we evaluate multiple families of representative LLMs and examine their robustness. Across 18 commercial and open-source models we observe sharp performance degradation on the variants. OpenAI's flagship reasoning model, O3, scores 51.5% on the originals but drops by 4.7 percentage points on surface-renaming variants, and by 12.9 percentage points on parametric variants, while smaller models fare far worse. Overall, the results show that the proposed new evaluation methodology is effective for deepening our understanding of the robustness of LLMs and generating new insights for further improving their mathematical reasoning capabilities.

</details>


### [34] [Semi-Supervised Synthetic Data Generation with Fine-Grained Relevance Control for Short Video Search Relevance Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.16717)
*Haoran Li,Zhiming Su,Junyan Yao,Enwei Zhang,Yang Ji,Yan Chen,Kan Zhou,Chao Feng,Jiao Ran*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于中文短视频的半监督合成数据生成方法，通过引入四级相关性标注，解决了现有方法在数据稀疏和领域特定分布捕捉方面的不足，并提升了嵌入模型的性能和在线推荐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于提示的合成数据方法在捕捉领域特定数据分布，尤其是在数据稀疏的领域，存在不足，并且往往忽略了细粒度的相关性多样性。这导致训练数据在相关性分布上不够均衡，影响了嵌入模型的性能。

Method: 本文提出了一种半监督合成数据生成流程。首先，构建了一个包含四级相关性标注的中文短视频数据集。然后，利用两个协同训练的模型生成领域自适应的短视频数据，并可控地生成相关性标签。该方法通过合成代表性不足的中级相关性样本来增强相关性级别的多样性，从而得到更均衡、语义更丰富的训练数据集。

Result: 离线实验表明，在合成数据上训练的嵌入模型优于基于提示生成数据或使用标准监督微调（SFT）的模型。在线 A/B 测试结果显示，在抖音双栏场景的搜索增强推荐流程中，所提出的模型将点击率（CTR）提升了 1.45%，强相关性比例（SRR）提高了 4.9%，图片用户渗透率（IUPR）提升了 0.1054%。

Conclusion: 本文提出的半监督合成数据方法能够生成具有细粒度相关性多样性的中文短视频数据，有效提升了嵌入模型的性能和在线推荐效果。研究强调了在嵌入学习中，细粒度相关性监督的价值，并为数据稀疏领域的合成数据生成提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Synthetic data is widely adopted in embedding models to ensure diversity in training data distributions across dimensions such as difficulty, length, and language. However, existing prompt-based synthesis methods struggle to capture domain-specific data distributions, particularly in data-scarce domains, and often overlook fine-grained relevance diversity. In this paper, we present a Chinese short video dataset with 4-level relevance annotations, filling a critical resource void. Further, we propose a semi-supervised synthetic data pipeline where two collaboratively trained models generate domain-adaptive short video data with controllable relevance labels. Our method enhances relevance-level diversity by synthesizing samples for underrepresented intermediate relevance labels, resulting in a more balanced and semantically rich training data set. Extensive offline experiments show that the embedding model trained on our synthesized data outperforms those using data generated based on prompting or vanilla supervised fine-tuning(SFT). Moreover, we demonstrate that incorporating more diverse fine-grained relevance levels in training data enhances the model's sensitivity to subtle semantic distinctions, highlighting the value of fine-grained relevance supervision in embedding learning. In the search enhanced recommendation pipeline of Douyin's dual-column scenario, through online A/B testing, the proposed model increased click-through rate(CTR) by 1.45%, raised the proportion of Strong Relevance Ratio (SRR) by 4.9%, and improved the Image User Penetration Rate (IUPR) by 0.1054%.

Method: 研究者收集了来自OpenStreetMap的真实GPS轨迹数据，并将其与上下文层（包括停靠点、移动、兴趣点、推断的交通方式和天气数据）相结合。他们还使用大型语言模型（LLM）生成了与轨迹相关的合成社交媒体帖子。构建的数据集提供了表格和RDF两种格式，以支持语义推理和FAIR数据原则。研究者还开源了一个可复现的流水线，允许用户自定义数据集。数据集覆盖了巴黎和纽约两个城市。

Result: 本文提出了两个包含丰富语义信息的人类轨迹数据集（巴黎和纽约），并提供了一个开源的流水线来构建这些数据集。数据集整合了真实轨迹、上下文信息（停靠点、POI、交通模式、天气）以及LLM生成的社交媒体帖子，支持多模态和语义分析。数据集以表格和RDF格式提供，符合FAIR数据原则。研究者强调，这是首个结合了真实移动数据、结构化语义信息、LLM文本和语义Web兼容性的可重用框架。

Conclusion: 本研究通过提供一个整合了真实轨迹、多维度语义信息和LLM生成文本的数据集，为人类移动性分析和LLM应用开辟了新的可能性。该数据集及其构建流水线的开放性，将促进相关领域的研究，并有望推动行为建模、移动性预测和知识图谱构建等方面的进展。未来的工作可以探索更复杂的LLM集成和更广泛的应用场景。

Abstract: In this resource paper, we present two publicly available datasets of semantically enriched human trajectories, together with the pipeline to build them. The trajectories are publicly available GPS traces retrieved from OpenStreetMap. Each dataset includes contextual layers such as stops, moves, points of interest (POIs), inferred transportation modes, and weather data. A novel semantic feature is the inclusion of synthetic, realistic social media posts generated by Large Language Models (LLMs), enabling multimodal and semantic mobility analysis. The datasets are available in both tabular and Resource Description Framework (RDF) formats, supporting semantic reasoning and FAIR data practices. They cover two structurally distinct, large cities: Paris and New York. Our open source reproducible pipeline allows for dataset customization, while the datasets support research tasks such as behavior modeling, mobility prediction, knowledge graph construction, and LLM-based applications. To our knowledge, our resource is the first to combine real-world movement, structured semantic enrichment, LLM-generated text, and semantic web compatibility in a reusable framework.

### [36] [HUME: Measuring the Human-Model Performance Gap in Text Embedding Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.10062)
*Adnan El Assadi,Isaac Chung,Roman Solomatin,Niklas Muennighoff,Kenneth Enevoldsen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了HUME框架，用于评估文本嵌入模型的性能，并首次提供了跨多种语言和任务的人类表现基线。研究发现，虽然最佳嵌入模型在某些任务上表现优于人类，但在低资源语言等任务上仍有差距。此外，研究还评估了大型语言模型作为标注者的表现，发现其未能达到人类水平。该研究为理解和改进嵌入模型提供了有价值的见解，并指出了现有数据集存在的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然文本嵌入模型在理解和处理语言方面取得了显著进展，但缺乏与人类表现的直接比较，使得对其能力和局限性的理解不完整。现有的模型评估框架（如MTEB）虽然广泛，但缺少可靠的人类表现基线，限制了模型得分的可解释性。因此，这项研究的动机是填补这一空白，通过提供跨多种语言和任务的人类表现数据，为评估嵌入模型提供一个更全面的视角，从而更好地指导模型的开发和改进。

Method: 该研究提出了HUME（Human Evaluation Framework for Text Embeddings）框架，旨在衡量人类在文本嵌入任务上的表现。研究人员在16个MTEB数据集上进行了实验，这些数据集涵盖了重排、分类、聚类和语义文本相似性等任务，并覆盖了高资源和低资源语言。通过设计相应的人类标注任务，收集了人类在这些任务上的表现数据，并将其作为基线。同时，研究还评估了九个大型语言模型（LLM）作为标注者在重排、分类和STS任务上的表现。

Result: 研究结果显示，在所有评估的任务和语言中，人类的平均表现达到77.6%，而最佳的嵌入模型平均表现为80.1%。然而，这种差距在不同数据集和语言上存在显著差异。在某些数据集上，模型表现优于人类，但在低资源语言等任务上，模型表现明显不如人类。此外，人类标注还揭示了现有数据集存在的一些问题。在作为标注者方面，大型语言模型的平均表现为76.1%，略低于人类的81.2%，尽管它们在可扩展性方面具有优势。

Conclusion: 这项研究成功地建立了人类在文本嵌入任务上的表现基线，并开发了一个可扩展的评估框架HUME。研究结果强调了在低资源语言和某些特定任务上，嵌入模型仍有提升空间，并指出了现有数据集的局限性。虽然大型语言模型在作为标注者方面显示出潜力，但其表现仍不及人类。该研究为嵌入模型的开发和评估提供了重要的参考，并为未来的研究指出了方向，包括开发更强大的模型，以及改进现有基准和创建更具挑战性的新数据集。

Abstract: Comparing human and model performance offers a valuable perspective for understanding the strengths and limitations of embedding models, highlighting where they succeed and where they fail to capture meaning and nuance. However, such comparisons are rarely made, as human performance on embedding tasks is difficult to measure. To fill this gap, we introduce HUME: Human Evaluation Framework for Text Embeddings. While frameworks like MTEB provide broad model evaluation, they lack reliable estimates of human performance, limiting the interpretability of model scores. We measure human performance across 16 MTEB datasets spanning reranking, classification, clustering, and semantic textual similarity across linguistically diverse high- and low-resource languages. Humans achieve an average performance of 77.6% compared to 80.1% for the best embedding model, though with substantial variation: models reach high performance on some datasets while struggling on notably low-resource languages. Our human annotations also reveal multiple dataset issues. We additionally benchmark nine LLMs as annotators on reranking, classification, and STS tasks, finding that they fall short of human performance (76.1% vs. 81.2%) despite offering scalability advantages. We provide human performance baselines, insights into task difficulty patterns, and an extensible evaluation framework that enables a more meaningful interpretation of results and informs the development of both models and benchmarks. Our code, dataset, and leaderboard are publicly available at https://github.com/embeddings-benchmark/mteb.

</details>


### [37] [ThaiOCRBench: A Task-Diverse Benchmark for Vision-Language Understanding in Thai](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04479)
*Surapon Nonesung,Teetouch Jaknamon,Sirinya Chaiophat,Natapong Nitarach,Chanakan Wittayasakpan,Warit Sirichotedumrong,Adisai Na-Thalang,Kunat Pipatanakul*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了ThaiOCRBench，首个用于评估视觉-语言模型（VLMs）在泰语富文本视觉理解任务上的综合基准。该基准包含2808个样本，覆盖13个任务类别，旨在解决现有基准对高资源语言的偏重问题。评估结果显示，专有模型（如Gemini 2.5 Pro）在零样本设置下优于开源模型，尤其在细粒度文本识别和手写内容提取方面，开源模型性能下降显著。错误分析揭示了语言偏见、结构不匹配和内容幻觉等挑战。ThaiOCRBench为评估低资源、脚本复杂环境下的VLMs提供了标准化框架，并为改进泰语文档理解提供了见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型（VLMs）的评估基准主要集中在高资源语言上，导致像泰语这样的低资源语言在文本丰富的视觉理解任务（尤其是在文档结构理解方面）的评估上存在显著不足。这阻碍了VLMs在泰语领域的应用和发展。

Method: 构建了一个名为ThaiOCRBench的全面基准，包含2808个人工标注的样本，覆盖13种不同的泰语视觉理解任务。然后，在零样本设置下，对包括专有模型（如Gemini 2.5 Pro）和开源模型在内的多种先进VLMs进行了评估。最后，通过详细的错误分析来识别模型在理解泰语文档时遇到的具体挑战。

Result: 在零样本评估中，专有模型（例如Gemini 2.5 Pro）普遍优于开源模型。在细粒度文本识别和手写内容提取等任务上，开源模型的性能下降尤为明显。错误分析表明，语言偏见、结构不匹配和模型生成幻觉是导致性能不佳的主要原因。

Conclusion: ThaiOCRBench填补了泰语在VLMs评估基准上的空白，为低资源、脚本复杂的语言环境提供了标准的评估框架。研究结果揭示了当前VLMs在处理泰语文档理解任务时存在的挑战，并为未来改进模型（特别是在克服语言偏见和提高结构理解能力方面）提供了重要的方向和依据。

Abstract: We present ThaiOCRBench, the first comprehensive benchmark for evaluating vision-language models (VLMs) on Thai text-rich visual understanding tasks. Despite recent progress in multimodal modeling, existing benchmarks predominantly focus on high-resource languages, leaving Thai underrepresented, especially in tasks requiring document structure understanding. ThaiOCRBench addresses this gap by offering a diverse, human-annotated dataset comprising 2,808 samples across 13 task categories. We evaluate a wide range of state-of-the-art VLMs in a zero-shot setting, spanning both proprietary and open-source systems. Results show a significant performance gap, with proprietary models (e.g., Gemini 2.5 Pro) outperforming open-source counterparts. Notably, fine-grained text recognition and handwritten content extraction exhibit the steepest performance drops among open-source models. Through detailed error analysis, we identify key challenges such as language bias, structural mismatch, and hallucinated content. ThaiOCRBench provides a standardized framework for assessing VLMs in low-resource, script-complex settings, and provides actionable insights for improving Thai-language document understanding.

### [38] [Evaluating Autoformalization Robustness via Semantically Similar Paraphrasing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.12784)
*Hayden Moore,Asfahan Shah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型（LLM）在自动形式化方面表现出巨大潜力，但其生成形式化证明的鲁棒性仍有待提高。本研究通过在MiniF2F和ProofNet基准上，使用两种现代LLM对经过释义的自然语言陈述进行评估，发现LLM对输入的微小语义变化非常敏感，导致生成证明的有效性和可编译性存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLM）在自动形式化领域取得了显著进展，但它们在生成经过验证且可靠的形式化证明方面仍面临挑战。先前在文本到SQL领域的研究表明，LLM对自然语言输入的释义非常敏感，即使语义高度保真，其性能也会受到影响。本研究旨在将这一发现扩展到自动形式化领域，评估LLM在处理经过释义的自然语言陈述时生成形式化证明的鲁棒性，以揭示其在理解和形式化复杂逻辑推理方面的潜在脆弱性。

Method: 本研究采用实验评估的方法，在MiniF2F和ProofNet（Lean 4版本）这两个正式的基准数据集上进行。研究使用了两种现代的大型语言模型。首先，对基准中的自然语言陈述进行释义，生成语义上相似但表述不同的输入。然后，利用这些释义后的陈述，分别在两个LLM上生成形式化证明。最后，通过测量生成证明的语义有效性和可编译性，跨模型对结果进行交叉评估，以量化LLM在面对输入变化时的性能变异性。

Result: 研究结果表明，大型语言模型在生成形式化证明时，对输入的自然语言陈述的微小变化表现出显著的敏感性。即使是语义上高度相似的释义输入，也可能导致模型生成证明的性能出现显著波动，具体体现在语义有效性和可编译性指标上。这种变异性表明，当前LLM在自动形式化任务中，其鲁棒性仍有待提高，模型输出的稳定性受到输入表达方式的影响。

Conclusion: 本研究证实了在自动形式化领域，大型语言模型（LLM）对于自然语言输入的释义是敏感的。研究结果揭示了模型性能的变异性，即输入语句的细微调整可能严重影响模型生成形式化证明的质量和有效性。这表明，在将LLM应用于需要高可靠性的形式化任务时，必须谨慎考虑输入的敏感性问题。未来的研究可以着眼于提高LLM对自然语言变异的鲁棒性，以及开发更可靠的评估方法来衡量其形式化能力。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently emerged as powerful tools for autoformalization. Despite their impressive performance, these models can still struggle to produce grounded and verifiable formalizations. Recent work in text-to-SQL, has revealed that LLMs can be sensitive to paraphrased natural language (NL) inputs, even when high degrees of semantic fidelity are preserved (Safarzadeh, Oroojlooyjadid, and Roth 2025). In this paper, we investigate this claim in the autoformalization domain. Specifically, we evaluate the robustness of LLMs generating formal proofs with semantically similar paraphrased NL statements by measuring semantic and compilation validity. Using the formal benchmarks MiniF2F (Zheng, Han, and Polu 2021) and Lean 4 version of ProofNet (Xin et al. 2024), and two modern LLMs, we generate paraphrased natural language statements and cross-evaluate these statements across both models. The results of this paper reveal performance variability across paraphrased inputs, demonstrating that minor shifts in NL statements can significantly impact model outputs.

</details>


### [39] [SeSE: A Structural Information-Guided Uncertainty Quantification Framework for Hallucination Detection in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.16275)
*Xingtao Zhao,Hao Peng,Dingli Su,Xianghua Zeng,Chunyang Liu,Jinzhi Liao,Philip S. Yu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了语义结构熵（SeSE），一种新的不确定性量化（UQ）框架，用于检测大型语言模型（LLMs）的“幻觉”。SeSE从结构信息角度量化LLMs的语义不确定性，与现有的基于概率或距离的方法不同，它利用了潜在的语义结构信息。该方法具有零资源、即插即用（off-the-shelf）的特点，适用于各种LLMs和任务。通过构建稀疏有向语义图和利用分层抽象，SeSE将不确定性定义为最优语义编码树的结构熵。实验证明，SeSE在29个模型-数据集组合上显著优于先进的UQ基线方法，并且可以扩展到对长文本生成中的单个声明进行细粒度UQ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在安全关键场景中部署大型语言模型（LLMs）需要可靠的不确定性量化（UQ），以便模型在不确定时能够避免生成“幻觉”般的错误信息。然而，现有的UQ方法主要依赖于语义概率分布或成对距离，忽略了可以提供更精确不确定性估计的潜在语义结构信息。因此，开发一种能够有效利用语义结构信息来量化LLM不确定性的新方法至关重要，以提高其在安全关键应用中的可靠性。

Method: 本研究提出了语义结构熵（SeSE）框架。首先，开发了一种自适应稀疏有向语义图构建算法，用于构建语义空间模型，该算法能够捕捉方向性语义依赖关系，并自动修剪不必要的连接。其次，通过分层抽象来利用潜在的语义结构信息：SeSE被定义为最优语义编码树的结构熵，量化了最优压缩后语义空间内的内在不确定性。更高的SeSE值表示更高的不确定性，预示着LLM更可能产生幻觉。此外，为了增强长文本生成的细粒度UQ，SeSE被扩展到通过对其随机语义交互进行建模来量化单个声明的不确定性。

Result: 通过在29个模型-数据集组合上进行的大量实验，SeSE被证明能够显著优于先进的UQ基线方法。该方法在不确定性量化和幻觉检测方面表现出卓越的性能。SeSE的扩展版本在长文本生成场景下，也能提供细粒度的不确定性度量，从而提高对单个声明的幻觉检测能力。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的语义结构熵（SeSE）框架为大型语言模型的不确定性量化提供了一种新颖且有效的方法，特别是在幻觉检测方面。SeSE利用语义结构信息，超越了传统基于概率或距离的方法。其零资源和即插即用的特性使其易于部署。虽然SeSE在实验中表现出色，但未来的工作可以进一步探索其在更广泛任务上的应用，并可能研究更复杂的语义结构建模技术以进一步提升性能。

Abstract: Reliable uncertainty quantification (UQ) is essential for deploying large language models (LLMs) in safety-critical scenarios, as it enables them to abstain from responding when uncertain, thereby avoiding ``hallucinating'' falsehoods. However, state-of-the-art UQ methods primarily rely on semantic probability distributions or pairwise distances, overlooking latent semantic structural information that could enable more precise uncertainty estimates. This paper presents Semantic Structural Entropy (SeSE), a principled UQ framework that quantifies the inherent semantic uncertainty of LLMs from a structural information perspective for hallucination detection. SeSE operates in a zero-resource manner and is applicable to both open- and closed-source LLMs, making it an ``off-the-shelf" solution for new models and tasks. Specifically, to effectively model semantic spaces, we first develop an adaptively sparsified directed semantic graph construction algorithm that captures directional semantic dependencies while automatically pruning unnecessary connections that introduce negative interference. We then exploit latent semantic structural information through hierarchical abstraction: SeSE is defined as the structural entropy of the optimal semantic encoding tree, formalizing intrinsic uncertainty within semantic spaces after optimal compression. A higher SeSE value corresponds to greater uncertainty, indicating that LLMs are highly likely to generate hallucinations. In addition, to enhance fine-grained UQ in long-form generation, we extend SeSE to quantify the uncertainty of individual claims by modeling their random semantic interactions, providing theoretically explicable hallucination detection. Extensive experiments across 29 model-dataset combinations show that SeSE significantly outperforms advanced UQ baselines.

</details>

### [40] [Complementary Characterization of Agent-Based Models via Computational Mechanics and Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04771)
*Roberto Garrone*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文将扩散模型作为一种新的工具，与ε-机器（ε-machines）相结合，用于表征和分析基于智能体模型（ABMs）的输出。ε-机器侧重于ABM生成时间序列的预测和计算结构，而扩散模型则专注于高维截面分布、数据流形学习和生成合成结果。研究表明，这两种方法在数学上是互补的，分别作用于“过程”和“分布”这两个不同的领域。将两者结合，可以从时间组织和分布几何两个维度来表示ABM的行为。这是首次将计算力学与基于得分的生成模型结合起来，用于ABM输出的结构分析，并将ABM表征置于现代机器学习方法（如密度估计和内在计算）的背景下。该框架通过使用一篇相关论文中介绍的长老-看护ABM数据集进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的ABM分析方法主要关注模型的时间动态和预测能力，但忽略了模型输出在高维空间中的分布结构。这种忽视可能导致对模型行为的理解不全面，尤其是在处理复杂的、多智能体交互产生的群体层面结果时。因此，需要一种能够同时捕捉ABM时间组织和分布几何特征的方法，以提供更全面的模型分析。

Method: 本文将扩散模型（diffusion models）作为一种新的工具，与已有的ε-机器（ε-machines）方法相结合，用于表征ABM的输出。ε-机器用于分析ABM生成时间序列的预测和计算结构，而扩散模型则用于表征ABM输出的高维截面分布，学习数据流形，并生成合成的群体层面结果。文章进行了形式分析，证明了ε-机器（作用于过程）和扩散模型（作用于分布）在数学上的互补性。该框架通过长老-看护ABM数据集进行了验证。

Result: 研究表明，ε-机器和扩散模型在分析ABM输出时具有互补性。ε-机器擅长捕捉时间序列的预测结构，而扩散模型则能有效表征高维分布几何。将两者结合，提供了一个二维的ABM行为表示，能够同时评估时间组织和分布结构。实验验证表明，该框架能够精确地定义和形式化ε-机器与扩散模型之间的互补性，为复杂模拟模型提供了一种原则性的联合分析方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个结合计算力学（ε-机器）和扩散模型的框架，用于联合分析ABM的时间可预测性和高维分布结构。该框架为ABM的表征提供了一种新颖且全面的方法，将ABM分析置于现代机器学习技术（如密度估计和内在计算）的更广阔背景中。通过在长老-看护ABM数据集上的验证，证明了该方法在提供对复杂模拟模型行为的深入理解方面的潜力。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在其他ABM应用中的适用性。

Abstract: This article extends the preprint "Characterizing Agent-Based Model Dynamics via $ε$-Machines and Kolmogorov-Style Complexity" by introducing diffusion models as orthogonal and complementary tools for characterizing the output of agent-based models (ABMs). Where $ε$-machines capture the predictive temporal structure and intrinsic computation of ABM-generated time series, diffusion models characterize high-dimensional cross-sectional distributions, learn underlying data manifolds, and enable synthetic generation of plausible population-level outcomes. We provide a formal analysis demonstrating that the two approaches operate on distinct mathematical domains -processes vs.\ distributions- and show that their combination yields a two-axis representation of ABM behavior based on temporal organization and distributional geometry. To our knowledge, this is the first framework to integrate computational mechanics with score-based generative modeling for the structural analysis of ABM outputs, thereby situating ABM characterization within the broader landscape of modern machine-learning methods for density estimation and intrinsic computation. The framework is validated using the same elder-caregiver ABM dataset introduced in the companion paper, and we provide precise definitions and propositions formalizing the mathematical complementarity between $ε$-machines and diffusion models. This establishes a principled methodology for jointly analyzing temporal predictability and high-dimensional distributional structure in complex simulation models.

### [41] [NAWOA-XGBoost: A Novel Model for Early Prediction of Academic Potential in Computer Science Students](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04751)
*Junhao Wei,Yanzhao Gu,Ran Zhang,Mingjing Huang,Jinhong Song,Yanxiao Li,Wenxuan Zhu,Yapeng Wang,Zikun Li,Zhiwen Wang,Xu Yang,Ngai Cheong*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为非线性自适应鲸鱼优化算法（NAWOA）的新型优化算法，以解决标准鲸鱼优化算法（WOA）在全局搜索能力、收敛速度和陷入局部最优方面存在的问题。NAWOA通过引入多种策略（如优质节点集初始化、领导者-追随者觅食、动态围捕猎物、三角形狩猎和非线性收敛因子）来增强其探索、利用和收敛稳定性。在基准函数测试中，NAWOA表现出优越的优化能力和鲁棒性。在此基础上，研究人员将NAWOA应用于XGBoost模型的超参数优化，构建了NAWOA-XGBoost模型，并使用2009-2019年澳门理工大学495名计算机科学本科生的数据来预测学术潜力。实验结果表明，NAWOA-XGBoost在准确率（0.8148）、宏F1（0.8101）、AUC（0.8932）和G-Mean（0.8172）等关键指标上均优于传统的XGBoost和WOA-XGBoost模型，证明了其在多类别不平衡数据集上的强大适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的鲸鱼优化算法（WOA）在应用于机器学习模型的超参数优化时，存在全局搜索能力有限、收敛速度慢以及容易陷入局部最优等缺点，这在很大程度上限制了其有效性。这些问题在处理复杂和高维的优化问题时尤为突出，例如机器学习模型的超参数调优，其中搜索空间可能非常广阔且充满局部最优解。因此，有必要改进WOA，以提高其在这些应用中的性能和鲁棒性，从而更好地解决实际问题，如提高模型的预测精度和泛化能力。

Method: 本研究提出了一种非线性自适应鲸鱼优化算法（NAWOA），以克服标准WOA的局限性。NAWOA引入了以下关键策略：1. 优质节点集初始化（Good Nodes Set initialization）：采用一种策略来初始化种群，旨在提供更好的初始搜索点。2. 领导者-追随者觅食（Leader-Followers Foraging）：模仿鲸鱼的捕食行为，引入领导者和追随者机制，以平衡算法的探索和利用能力。3. 动态围捕猎物（Dynamic Encircling Prey）：动态调整围捕猎物的策略，以适应不同阶段的搜索需求。4. 三角形狩猎（Triangular Hunting）：引入一种新的搜索模式，可能有助于跳出局部最优。5. 非线性收敛因子（nonlinear convergence factor）：采用非线性变化的收敛因子，以控制算法的收敛速度和稳定性。在算法性能验证方面，研究人员在23个基准函数上对NAWOA进行了测试，以评估其优化能力和鲁棒性。随后，将NAWOA应用于XGBoost模型的超参数优化，构建了NAWOA-XGBoost模型，并使用澳门理工大学2009-2019年495名计算机科学本科生的数据进行了学术潜力预测实验。实验设置包括与传统XGBoost和WOA-XGBoost模型进行性能比较。

Result: 在23个基准函数测试中，NAWOA展现出优越的优化能力和鲁棒性，证明了其在解决通用优化问题上的有效性。在学术潜力预测任务中，NAWOA-XGBoost模型取得了显著的成果。与传统的XGBoost和WOA-XGBoost模型相比，NAWOA-XGBoost在多个关键评估指标上均表现更优：准确率（Accuracy）达到了0.8148，宏F1得分（Macro F1）为0.8101，AUC值为0.8932，G-Mean得分为0.8172。这些结果表明，NAWOA在超参数优化方面能够有效地提升XGBoost模型的性能，尤其是在处理多类别不平衡数据集时，其适应性和有效性得到了充分体现。

Conclusion: 本研究成功提出并验证了一种名为非线性自适应鲸鱼优化算法（NAWOA）的新型优化算法，有效解决了标准鲸鱼优化算法（WOA）在全局搜索、收敛速度和局部最优问题上的不足。NAWOA通过整合多种创新策略，在基准函数测试中显示出优越的优化能力和鲁棒性。更重要的是，将NAWOA应用于XGBoost模型的超参数优化，构建的NAWOA-XGBoost模型在预测澳门理工大学计算机科学本科生学术潜力方面取得了优异的性能，显著优于传统XGBoost和WOA-XGBoost模型。该研究证明了NAWOA在处理多类别不平衡数据集上的强大适应性，为机器学习模型的超参数优化提供了有效的新方法。未来的工作可以进一步探索NAWOA在其他更广泛领域的应用，并考虑进一步优化算法结构或结合其他元启发式算法的优点。

Abstract: Whale Optimization Algorithm (WOA) suffers from limited global search ability, slow convergence, and tendency to fall into local optima, restricting its effectiveness in hyperparameter optimization for machine learning models. To address these issues, this study proposes a Nonlinear Adaptive Whale Optimization Algorithm (NAWOA), which integrates strategies such as Good Nodes Set initialization, Leader-Followers Foraging, Dynamic Encircling Prey, Triangular Hunting, and a nonlinear convergence factor to enhance exploration, exploitation, and convergence stability. Experiments on 23 benchmark functions demonstrate NAWOA's superior optimization capability and robustness. Based on this optimizer, an NAWOA-XGBoost model was developed to predict academic potential using data from 495 Computer Science undergraduates at Macao Polytechnic University (2009-2019). Results show that NAWOA-XGBoost outperforms traditional XGBoost and WOA-XGBoost across key metrics, including Accuracy (0.8148), Macro F1 (0.8101), AUC (0.8932), and G-Mean (0.8172), demonstrating strong adaptability on multi-class imbalanced datasets.

</details>


### [42] [Customer Identification for Electricity Retailers Based on Monthly Demand Profiles by Activity Sectors and Locations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04776)
*Joaquin Luque,Alejandro Carrasco,Enrique Personal,Francisco Perez,Carlos Leon*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: In the competitive electric sector, retail companies struggle to attract profitable customers due to anonymized energy demand data. This paper uses economic sector and location data from a large Spanish dataset (millions of monthly demand profiles) to indirectly identify customers. A KPI based on demand profile distance from target profiles is developed for a marketing strategy. The method uniquely identified 100,000 customers and identified 300,000 others in small sets. The strategy reduced distance from the target by 40% for 10,000 new customers compared to random attraction.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The electric sector faces increasing competition, forcing retail companies to strategically attract the most profitable customers. Profitability is often determined by how well a customer's energy demand profile aligns with specific target profiles, which are influenced by generation or cost policies. However, energy demand data is typically anonymized, preventing direct customer identification and thus hindering targeted marketing efforts. This research addresses the challenge of indirectly identifying customers using available, albeit anonymized, data to enable effective customer acquisition strategies.

Method: This study utilizes a large dataset comprising millions of monthly energy demand profiles from Spain. To overcome the anonymity of demand data, the researchers leverage associated information, specifically the economic sector and geographical location of the customers. They define a Key Performance Indicator (KPI) based on the 'distance' of a customer's demand profile from predefined target profiles. This KPI serves as the primary driver for their proposed marketing strategy, which aims to indirectly identify and target customers. The effectiveness of this identification method is evaluated by the number of uniquely identified customers and the size of the identifiable sets.

Result: The application of activity (economic sector) and location data enabled the indirect identification of a significant number of customers. Specifically, 100,000 customers were uniquely identified. An additional 300,000 customers were identified within small, manageable sets, each containing 10 or fewer consumers. To evaluate the marketing strategy, it was compared against a baseline of randomly attracting new clients. The proposed strategy demonstrated a substantial improvement, achieving a 40% reduction in the distance from the target profile for 10,000 newly acquired customers.

Conclusion: The research successfully demonstrates that combining economic sector and location data is a powerful method for the indirect identification of electric utility customers, overcoming the challenge posed by anonymized demand profiles. The developed KPI and resulting marketing strategy significantly outperform random customer acquisition, leading to a marked improvement in attracting customers whose demand aligns with profitability targets. While the study identified a large number of customers, limitations may exist in the granularity of identification for all remaining customers. Future work could explore refining the identification techniques or incorporating additional data sources to further enhance customer segmentation and marketing efficacy.

Abstract: The increasing competition in the electric sector is challenging retail companies as they must assign its commercial efforts to attract the most profitable customers. Those are whose energy demand best fit certain target profiles, which usually depend on generation or cost policies. But, even when the demand profile is available, it is in an anonymous way, preventing its association to a particular client. In this paper, we explore a large dataset containing several millions of monthly demand profiles in Spain and use the available information about the associated economic sector and location for an indirect identification of the customers. The distance of the demand profile from the target is used to define a key performance indicator (KPI) which is used as the main driver of the proposed marketing strategy. The combined use of activity and location has been revealed as a powerful tool for indirect identification of customers, as 100,000 customers are uniquely identified, while about 300,000 clients are identifiable in small sets containing 10 or less consumers. To assess the proposed marketing strategy, it has been compared to the random attraction of new clients, showing a reduction of distance from the target of 40% for 10,000 new customers.

### [43] [AI-Assisted Game Management Decisions: A Fuzzy Logic Approach to Real-Time Substituitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04480)
*Pedro Passos*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于模糊逻辑的决策支持系统（DSS），用于优化精英足球比赛中的实时换人决策。该系统通过改进的 PlayeRank 指标、生理指标和战术变量，克服了传统方法依赖直觉或易受偏见影响的局限性，实现了比黑箱模型更透明、可解释且有效的换人建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精英足球比赛中的换人决策对球队的经济和体育成绩有着重大影响，但现有决策方式（依赖直觉或模仿历史偏见的预测模型）存在不足。传统机器学习方法在试图复制人类行为时会遇到预测瓶颈。因此，需要一种更客观、可解释且能实时指导比赛管理的决策支持系统。

Method: 本研究提出了一种基于模糊逻辑的决策支持系统（DSS）。核心方法包括：1. 改进 PlayeRank 指标，提出累积均值与角色感知归一化（Cumulative Mean with Role Aware Normalization），以消除累积和模型中固有的比赛时间暴露偏差，实现准确的比赛内部比较。2. 整合改进后的指标与生理指标（如疲劳度）和情境变量（如由战术角色决定的纪律风险）。3. 基于上述信息计算动态换人优先度（P final）。4. 通过对 2018 年 FIFA 世界杯巴西对阵比利时比赛的案例研究进行验证。

Result: 案例研究结果显示，该系统具有生态效度。在换人建议方面，系统与专家共识（例如关于加布里埃尔·热苏斯的换人）一致，并且能够识别出人类决策者忽略的高风险场景。具体而言，该模型在关键黄牌出现前几分钟就预警了“FAGNER 悖论”（最高优先级的防守风险），并检测到“卢卡库悖论”（孤立的助攻掩盖了参与度的严重下降）。

Conclusion: 模糊逻辑为优化实时战术决策提供了一种透明、可解释且优于黑箱模型的选择。该 DSS 系统能够有效识别和管理比赛中的关键风险，为精英足球的战术决策提供有价值的辅助。未来工作可进一步探索该系统的应用范围和集成其他数据源的可能性。

Abstract: In elite soccer, substitution decisions entail significant financial and sporting consequences yet remain heavily reliant on intuition or predictive models that merely mimic historical biases. This paper introduces a Fuzzy Logic based Decision Support System (DSS) designed for real time, prescriptive game management. Unlike traditional Machine Learning approaches that encounter a predictive ceiling by attempting to replicate human behavior, our system audits performance through an objective, rule based inference engine. We propose a methodological advancement by reformulating the PlayeRank metric into a Cumulative Mean with Role Aware Normalization, eliminating the play time exposure bias inherent in cumulative sum models to enable accurate intra match comparison. The system integrates this refined metric with physiological proxies (fatigue) and contextual variables (disciplinary risk modulated by tactical role) to calculate a dynamic Substitution Priority (P final). Validation via a case study of the 2018 FIFA World Cup match between Brazil and Belgium demonstrates the system's ecological validity: it not only aligned with expert consensus on executed substitutions (for example Gabriel Jesus) but, crucially, identified high risk scenarios ignored by human decision makers. Specifically, the model flagged the "FAGNER Paradox" - a maximum priority defensive risk - minutes before a critical yellow card, and detected the "Lukaku Paradox", where an isolated assist masked a severe drop in participation. These results confirm that Fuzzy Logic offers a transparent, explainable, and superior alternative to black box models for optimizing real time tactical decisions.

### [44] [Solving N-Queen Problem using Las Vegas Algorithm with State Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04139)
*Susmita Sharma,Aayush Shrestha,Sitasma Thapa,Prashant Timalsina,Prakash Poudyal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: N皇后问题是一个经典的约束满足问题。传统的回溯法虽然能保证找到解，但时间复杂度高，不适用于大规模问题。基于Las Vegas算法的随机方法速度更快，但性能不稳定。本研究提出一种混合算法，通过迭代剪枝在Las Vegas算法框架下动态消除无效放置，有效减小了搜索空间。实验结果表明，该混合算法比传统回溯法在处理大规模N时性能更优，能更快地生成有效解，尤其适用于需要快速获得单一解的场景，并在计算成本和解的准确性之间取得了良好的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: N皇后问题虽然经典，但现有算法在处理大规模问题时面临挑战。完全方法（如回溯法）虽然能保证找到解，但时间复杂度呈指数级增长，不具备实用性。而随机方法（如Las Vegas算法）虽然速度更快，但其性能的随机性导致结果不稳定。因此，需要一种能够在大规模N皇后问题中提供快速且稳定解决方案的方法，这对于资源受限的计算环境尤为重要。

Method: 本研究提出了一种基于标准Las Vegas算法框架的混合算法。该算法的核心在于引入了“迭代剪枝”技术，在随机分配棋子的过程中动态地识别并消除无效的放置位置。通过这种方式，算法能够主动地缩小搜索空间，避免了不必要的计算。具体实验设置包括与传统回溯法进行性能对比，以评估其在不同规模N下的效率。

Result: 实验结果显示，传统的基于回溯的算法随着N的增大，性能急剧下降，扩展性较差。相比之下，本研究提出的混合算法在处理大规模N时，能够更稳定、更快速地生成有效的N皇后解决方案。尽管在N非常大的情况下，算法的性能仍可能存在一定的波动，但其整体表现显著优于传统回溯法，证明了其在提供及时解决方案方面的优越性。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发了一种结合了Las Vegas算法和迭代剪枝技术的混合算法，有效解决了N皇后问题在大规模实例中的效率和稳定性问题。该算法通过动态减小搜索空间，实现了计算成本和解的准确性之间的良好权衡，特别适用于需要在资源受限环境中快速获得高质量解的应用场景。未来的工作可以进一步探索优化剪枝策略，以应对更大规模的问题，并研究其在其他约束满足问题中的泛化能力。

Abstract: The N-Queens problem, placing all N queens in a N x N chessboard where none attack the other, is a classic problem for constraint satisfaction algorithms. While complete methods like backtracking guarantee a solution, their exponential time complexity makes them impractical for large-scale instances thus, stochastic approaches, such as Las Vegas algorithm, are preferred. While it offers faster approximate solutions, it suffers from significant performance variance due to random placement of queens on the board. This research introduces a hybrid algorithm built on top of the standard Las Vegas framework through iterative pruning, dynamically eliminating invalid placements during the random assignment phase, thus this method effectively reduces the search space. The analysis results that traditional backtracking scales poorly with increasing N. In contrast, the proposed technique consistently generates valid solutions more rapidly, establishing it as a superior alternative to use where a single, timely solution is preferred over completeness. Although large N causes some performance variability, the algorithm demonstrates a highly effective trade-off between computational cost and solution fidelity, making it particularly suited for resource-constrained computing environments.

### [45] [RippleBench: Capturing Ripple Effects Using Existing Knowledge Repositories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04144)
*Roy Rinberg,Usha Bhalla,Igor Shilov,Flavio P. Calmon,Rohit Gandikota*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为RippleBench-Maker的自动化工具，用于生成问答数据集，以衡量语言模型干预（如知识遗忘）中的“涟漪效应”（即对非目标信息的意外影响）。研究人员使用该工具构建了一个名为RippleBench-Bio的生物医学领域基准测试集，并评估了八种先进的遗忘方法，发现所有方法在遗忘目标知识时，都会对语义距离不同的相关知识产生准确率下降，且下降模式各不相同。研究团队开源了该工具和基准测试集，以支持未来的相关研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管针对语言模型的知识遗忘、去偏见或模型编辑等干预措施旨在精确修改模型行为和更新知识，但这些干预往往会波及到相关的、非预期的领域，即所谓的“涟漪效应”。这种效应阻碍了对模型干预效果的准确评估，并可能导致模型在其他方面的性能下降。因此，需要一种系统性的方法来量化和理解这种涟漪效应，以提高模型干预的可靠性和有效性。

Method: 研究人员开发了一个名为RippleBench-Maker的自动化工具，该工具利用基于维基百科的检索增强生成（RAG）流水线（WikiRAG）来生成多项选择题。这些问题围绕目标概念（即被遗忘的知识）在不同语义距离上进行设计。通过将RippleBench-Maker应用于WMDP（大规模杀伤性武器论文）数据集（一个常用的遗忘基准），研究人员构建了RippleBench-Bio，一个专注于生物医学领域的基准测试集。随后，他们使用这个基准测试集评估了八种最先进的遗忘方法，并分析了这些方法在不同语义距离上的准确率下降情况，以揭示其涟漪效应的传播模式。

Result: 通过在RippleBench-Bio基准测试集上评估八种先进的遗忘方法，研究发现所有方法都表现出非平凡的准确率下降。这种准确率下降的程度随着问题与被遗忘知识的语义距离的增加而增大。重要的是，每种遗忘方法都展现出独特的涟漪效应传播模式，表明其对不同相关知识领域的影响程度和方式存在差异。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发并验证了RippleBench-Maker工具和RippleBench-Bio基准测试集，为量化语言模型干预中的涟漪效应提供了一个有效框架。研究结果表明，当前的遗忘方法普遍存在涟漪效应，且其影响模式因方法而异。这项工作通过提供可量化的评估手段和相关的基准测试，为理解和缓解语言模型中的涟漪效应提供了重要支持，并为未来开发更具鲁棒性和可控性的模型干预技术奠定了基础。研究团队已将代码和基准测试集开源，以促进社区的进一步研究。

Abstract: Targeted interventions on language models, such as unlearning, debiasing, or model editing, are a central method for refining model behavior and keeping knowledge up to date. While these interventions aim to modify specific information within models (e.g., removing virology content), their effects often propagate to related but unintended areas (e.g., allergies); these side-effects are commonly referred to as the ripple effect. In this work, we present RippleBench-Maker, an automatic tool for generating Q&A datasets that allow for the measurement of ripple effects in any model-editing task. RippleBench-Maker builds on a Wikipedia-based RAG pipeline (WikiRAG) to generate multiple-choice questions at varying semantic distances from the target concept (e.g., the knowledge being unlearned). Using this framework, we construct RippleBench-Bio, a benchmark derived from the WMDP (Weapons of Mass Destruction Paper) dataset, a common unlearning benchmark. We evaluate eight state-of-the-art unlearning methods and find that all exhibit non-trivial accuracy drops on topics increasingly distant from the unlearned knowledge, each with distinct propagation profiles. To support ongoing research, we release our codebase for on-the-fly ripple evaluation, along with the benchmark, RippleBench-Bio.

</details>

Method: 本文提出并描述了Nemosine框架，一个基于模块化认知架构的设计。该架构的核心是功能性认知模块，称为“角色”（personas），每个角色负责特定的认知任务，如规划、评估、交叉检查和叙事综合。框架整合了元认知、分布式认知和模块化认知系统的原理。其设计通过形式化规范、内部一致性标准和可重复的结构组件进行文档化，以确保其清晰性和可实现性。

Conclusion: Nemosine框架作为一个模块化的认知架构，为支持辅助推理、结构化思维和系统性分析提供了一个创新的解决方案。它通过整合多种认知科学原理和采用模块化设计，为解决复杂问题和支持决策提供了有力的概念基础。未来的工作可以集中于该框架的具体计算实现，并进一步探索其在不同应用领域中的潜力，特别是在符号-模块化推理架构的研究方面。

Abstract: This paper presents the Nemosine Framework, a modular cognitive architecture designed to support assisted reasoning, structured thinking, and systematic analysis. The model operates through functional cognitive modules ("personas") that organize tasks such as planning, evaluation, cross-checking, and narrative synthesis. The framework combines principles from metacognition, distributed cognition, and modular cognitive systems to offer an operational structure for assisted problem-solving and decision support. The architecture is documented through formal specification, internal consistency criteria, and reproducible structural components. The goal is to provide a clear conceptual basis for future computational implementations and to contribute to the study of symbolic-modular architectures for reasoning.

TL;DR: Unlike most primary headaches, secondary headaches require specialized care and can have severe consequences if not promptly treated. Clinical guidelines identify "red flag" symptoms, but identifying patients needing urgent evaluation in primary care remains difficult due to time constraints, incomplete information, and varied presentations. This paper introduces a multi-agent LLM clinical decision support system, using an orchestrator-specialist architecture, to diagnose secondary headaches from clinical notes. The system uses seven specialized agents and a central orchestrator for task management. Tested on 90 expert-validated cases against single-LLM baselines and two prompting strategies (QPrompt, GPrompt), the multi-agent system with GPrompt and smaller LLMs showed the highest F1 scores, demonstrating that structured multi-agent reasoning improves accuracy beyond prompt engineering and provides a transparent, explainable approach for secondary headache diagnosis.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Clinicians often face time pressures, limited information, and a wide spectrum of patient symptoms, which can result in under-diagnosis and suboptimal treatment for secondary headaches. The research addresses this critical gap by developing an advanced decision support system to aid clinicians in accurately identifying secondary headaches.

Method: The study proposes a multi-agent large language model (LLM) based clinical decision support system employing an orchestrator-specialist architecture. This system is designed to provide explicit and interpretable diagnoses for secondary headaches by processing free-text clinical vignettes. The diagnostic process is broken down into tasks handled by seven domain-specialized agents, each generating a structured, evidence-based rationale. A central orchestrator manages task decomposition and directs the agents. The system

Result: The multi-agent system was evaluated using 90 expert-validated cases of secondary headaches. Notably, the performance gains were more pronounced with smaller LLMs, suggesting that the structured reasoning approach is particularly beneficial for less powerful models. The study demonstrated that this multi-agent approach enhances diagnostic accuracy beyond what can be achieved through prompt engineering alone.

Conclusion: The research successfully demonstrates that a structured multi-agent reasoning approach, implemented via an orchestrator-specialist architecture, significantly improves the accuracy of secondary headache diagnosis from clinical text compared to single-LLM baselines. Abstract: Unlike most primary headaches, secondary headaches need specialized care and can have devastating consequences if not treated promptly. Clinical guidelines highlight several 'red flag' features, such as thunderclap onset, meningismus, papilledema, focal neurologic deficits, signs of temporal arteritis, systemic illness, and the 'worst headache of their life' presentation. We present a large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent clinical decision support system built on an orchestrator-specialist architecture, designed to perform explicit and interpretable secondary headache diagnosis from free-text clinical vignettes. We evaluated the multi-agent system using 90 expert-validated secondary headache cases and compared its performance with a single-LLM baseline across two prompting strategies: question-based prompting (QPrompt) and clinical practice guideline-based prompting (GPrompt). ### [48] [Balancing Safety and Helpfulness in Healthcare AI Assistants through Iterative Preference Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04210)
*Huy Nghiem,Swetasudha Panda,Devashish Khatwani,Huy V. Nguyen,Krishnaram Kenthapadi,Hal Daumé*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种迭代的、部署后的对齐框架，结合KTO和DPO技术，以提高医疗领域大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全性和可信度。通过在CARES-18K基准上对四个LLMs进行评估，发现该框架能显著提升有害查询的检测率（最高可达42%），并揭示了与模型架构相关的校准偏差。研究还探讨了自我评估的可靠性，并强调了在设计对话式医疗助手时平衡患者安全、用户信任和临床效用的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在医疗领域的应用日益广泛，但其安全性与可信度问题是阻碍其大规模部署的关键障碍。对话式医疗助手需要在避免不安全合规的同时，减少对良性查询的过度拒绝。因此，研究旨在解决如何有效提升LLMs在医疗场景下的安全性和可靠性问题，以促进其在临床中的应用。

Method: 本研究提出了一种迭代的、部署后的对齐框架，利用Kahneman-Tversky Optimization (KTO) 和 Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) 技术来针对特定领域的安全信号优化模型。实验在CARES-18K基准上进行，评估了Llama-3B/8B、Meditron-8B和Mistral-7B四种大型语言模型在多轮迭代中的表现。此外，还进行了消融研究，以确定自我评估的有效性，以及何时需要外部或微调的评估者来最大化性能提升。

Result: 研究结果显示，该对齐框架在有害查询检测的安全相关指标方面取得了最高42%的改进。同时，在错误拒绝方面也观察到了有趣的权衡，并揭示了与模型架构相关的校准偏差。消融研究表明，在某些情况下，自我评估是可靠的，而在其他情况下，则需要外部或微调的评估者来获得最佳性能。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的迭代式部署后对齐框架，通过结合KTO和DPO技术，能够显著提升医疗领域大型语言模型的安全性和可靠性。研究结果强调了在设计对话式医疗助手时，平衡患者安全、用户信任和临床效用的重要性，并为未来研究提供了关于模型校准、评估策略和最佳实践的见解。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in healthcare, yet ensuring their safety and trustworthiness remains a barrier to deployment. Conversational medical assistants must avoid unsafe compliance without over-refusing benign queries. We present an iterative post-deployment alignment framework that applies Kahneman-Tversky Optimization (KTO) and Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) to refine models against domain-specific safety signals. Using the CARES-18K benchmark for adversarial robustness, we evaluate four LLMs (Llama-3B/8B, Meditron-8B, Mistral-7B) across multiple cycles. Our results show up to 42% improvement in safety-related metrics for harmful query detection, alongside interesting trade-offs against erroneous refusals, thereby exposing architecture-dependent calibration biases. We also perform ablation studies to identify when self-evaluation is reliable and when external or finetuned judges are necessary to maximize performance gains. Our findings underscore the importance of adopting best practices that balance patient safety, user trust, and clinical utility in the design of conversational medical assistants.

### [49] [Educational Cone Model in Embedding Vector Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04227)
*Yo Ehara*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为“教育圆锥模型”的几何框架，用于评估用于教育文本难度分析的嵌入方法。该模型基于“越简单的文本在嵌入空间中越不分散，越难的文本越分散”的假设，形成圆锥状分布，从而将嵌入评估转化为优化问题。通过设计损失函数，实现了避免计算成本的闭式解。实验证明该模型能有效且快速地识别出最适合难度标注教育文本的嵌入空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能教育系统需要包含难度评级的人工标注数据集。尽管嵌入向量空间在表示文本语义相似度方面被广泛应用且在文本难度分析方面显示出潜力，但大量的嵌入方法给选择最合适的方法带来了挑战。

Method: 提出教育圆锥模型，一个几何框架。该模型基于“越简单的文本越不分散（侧重于基础概念），越难的文本越分散”的假设。该假设导致嵌入空间中形成圆锥状分布，无论使用何种嵌入方法。该模型将嵌入的评估构建为一个优化问题，旨在检测基于结构化难度的模式。通过设计特定的损失函数，导出了避免昂贵计算的高效闭式解。

Result: 在真实世界数据集上的实证测试验证了该模型在识别与难度标注的教育文本最匹配的嵌入空间的有效性和速度。

Conclusion: 教育圆锥模型提供了一种新颖的几何方法来评估教育文本难度分析的嵌入方法。它将嵌入评估转化为优化问题，并通过高效的闭式解实现了快速准确的识别。该模型在真实数据集上的有效性得到了验证，为智能教育系统的发展提供了有价值的工具。未来的工作可以探索该模型在其他教育应用中的潜力，并进一步优化其计算效率。

Abstract: Human-annotated datasets with explicit difficulty ratings are essential in intelligent educational systems. Although embedding vector spaces are widely used to represent semantic closeness and are promising for analyzing text difficulty, the abundance of embedding methods creates a challenge in selecting the most suitable method. This study proposes the Educational Cone Model, which is a geometric framework based on the assumption that easier texts are less diverse (focusing on fundamental concepts), whereas harder texts are more diverse. This assumption leads to a cone-shaped distribution in the embedding space regardless of the embedding method used. The model frames the evaluation of embeddings as an optimization problem with the aim of detecting structured difficulty-based patterns. By designing specific loss functions, efficient closed-form solutions are derived that avoid costly computation. Empirical tests on real-world datasets validated the model's effectiveness and speed in identifying the embedding spaces that are best aligned with difficulty-annotated educational texts.

</details>


### [50] [Detecting Perspective Shifts in Multi-agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.05013)
*Eric Bridgeford,Hayden Helm*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Generative agents enhanced with external tools and update mechanisms ("agents") are increasingly used. Dynamic multi-agent systems are emerging, and current research focuses on single-time-point representations. This paper introduces the Temporal Data Kernel Perspective Space (TDKPS) for joint agent embedding over time. It proposes novel hypothesis tests to detect behavioral changes in black-box multi-agent systems at both individual and group levels. The paper analyzes the empirical properties of these tests, including hyperparameter sensitivity, using simulations of evolving digital personas. Furthermore, a natural experiment demonstrates that these tests can detect changes that correlate significantly and specifically with real external events. TDKPS is presented as the first principled framework for monitoring behavioral dynamics in black-box multi-agent systems, addressing a critical need as generative agent deployment expands.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The proliferation of generative agents augmented with external tools and update mechanisms has led to the natural emergence of dynamic multi-agent systems. Existing research has primarily focused on analyzing these systems using low-dimensional representations of agents based on query responses at a single time point. However, this approach is insufficient for understanding the temporal dynamics and behavioral changes within these systems. The significance of this research lies in the need for robust methods to monitor and detect behavioral shifts in black-box multi-agent systems, which is crucial as the deployment and scale of generative agents continue to grow. Without such monitoring capabilities, it becomes difficult to ensure system stability, identify anomalies, and understand the evolving interactions within these complex systems.

Method: The paper introduces the Temporal Data Kernel Perspective Space (TDKPS) as a novel framework for jointly embedding agents across time. This approach allows for the analysis of temporal dynamics in multi-agent systems. Building upon TDKPS, the researchers propose several new hypothesis tests designed to detect behavioral changes at both the individual agent level and the group level within black-box multi-agent systems. The empirical properties of these proposed tests are characterized, with a specific focus on their sensitivity to key hyperparameters. To evaluate their methods, the paper employs simulations that are motivated by a multi-agent system comprised of evolving digital personas. Additionally, a natural experiment is conducted to demonstrate the practical applicability and effectiveness of the proposed tests in real-world scenarios.

Result: The paper

Conclusion: The Temporal Data Kernel Perspective Space (TDKPS) framework and its associated hypothesis tests offer a principled and effective solution for monitoring behavioral dynamics in black-box multi-agent systems. The empirical analysis demonstrates the sensitivity of these tests to hyperparameters, and the simulations with evolving digital personas provide a controlled environment for evaluating their performance. Critically, the natural experiment showcases the ability of the proposed tests to detect changes that correlate sensitively, specifically, and significantly with real-world exogenous events. As generative agent deployment continues to scale, TDKPS represents a significant advancement, providing a much-needed capability for understanding and managing the complex evolving behaviors within these systems. Future work could explore extensions of TDKPS to different types of agent interactions, investigate more sophisticated anomaly detection techniques, and apply the framework to a wider range of real-world multi-agent applications.

Abstract: Generative models augmented with external tools and update mechanisms (or \textit{agents}) have demonstrated capabilities beyond intelligent prompting of base models. As agent use proliferates, dynamic multi-agent systems have naturally emerged. Recent work has investigated the theoretical and empirical properties of low-dimensional representations of agents based on query responses at a single time point. This paper introduces the Temporal Data Kernel Perspective Space (TDKPS), which jointly embeds agents across time, and proposes several novel hypothesis tests for detecting behavioral change at the agent- and group-level in black-box multi-agent systems. We characterize the empirical properties of our proposed tests, including their sensitivity to key hyperparameters, in simulations motivated by a multi-agent system of evolving digital personas. Finally, we demonstrate via natural experiment that our proposed tests detect changes that correlate sensitively, specifically, and significantly with a real exogenous event. As far as we are aware, TDKPS is the first principled framework for monitoring behavioral dynamics in black-box multi-agent systems -- a critical capability as generative agent deployment continues to scale.

### [51] [Addressing Logical Fallacies In Scientific Reasoning From Large Language Models: Towards a Dual-Inference Training Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04228)
*Peter B. Walker,Hannah Davidson,Aiden Foster,Matthew Lienert,Thomas Pardue,Dale Russell*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文指出，当前大型语言模型（LLMs）主要依赖“肯定式推理”（如“modus ponens”），这使得它们在面对否定、反例或错误前提时存在系统性弱点。为解决此问题，研究提出了一种“双重推理”训练框架，通过结合肯定式生成与结构化的反事实否定，使模型不仅能进行有效推理，还能识别并拒绝无效推理，从而提高模型的鲁棒性、可解释性和与人类推理的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型（LLMs）在自然语言处理领域取得了显著进展，并在科学、医疗和决策制定等领域展现出巨大潜力。然而，它们的训练模式主要基于“肯定式推理”，即从已接受的前提推导出预期的结论（类似于“modus ponens”）。尽管这种方式有助于生成流畅的文本，但它使得模型容易受到逻辑谬误、对抗性攻击以及因果推理失败的影响。特别是在科学推理中，模型在处理否定、反例或错误前提时会暴露出生系统的弱点。因此，研究的动机在于克服LLMs在逻辑推理方面的局限性，提升其在复杂推理任务中的可靠性和准确性。

Method: 本研究提出了一个“双重推理”训练框架。该框架在形式逻辑、认知科学和对抗性训练的基础上，将“否定前件”（denying the antecedent）的形式化，作为一种有效的“否证”和增强模型鲁棒性的机制。具体而言，该框架通过结合生成式综合与明确的、感知否定的目标，使模型能够同时进行肯定式生成和结构化的反事实否定。实验部分通过在科学推理领域（涉及医学和环境科学）对现有主流LLMs进行评估，展示了它们在处理否定、反例或错误前提时的系统性弱点，以此为基础引入并验证了所提出的双重推理训练框架的有效性。

Result: 实验表明，现有的LLMs在处理涉及否定、反例或错误前提的科学推理任务时，表现出系统性的推理缺陷。通过引入“双重推理”训练框架，模型在结合肯定式生成与结构化反事实否定后，能够有效识别并拒绝无效的推理。这使得模型在面对复杂的逻辑挑战时，展现出更高的鲁棒性和准确性，能够更好地进行因果推理，并且与人类的推理方式更加一致。

Conclusion: 本研究成功地展示了现有LLMs在处理否定性逻辑推理时的局限性，并提出了一种创新的“双重推理”训练框架。该框架通过融合肯定式推理和反事实否定，显著增强了LLMs的鲁棒性、可解释性和与人类推理的一致性。这项工作为开发更强大、更可靠的AI系统提供了新的途径，尤其是在对逻辑严谨性要求极高的科学和医疗等领域具有重要的实际意义和应用前景。未来的工作可以进一步探索该框架在更多复杂推理场景下的应用，以及优化其训练效率。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed natural language processing and hold growing promise for advancing science, healthcare, and decision-making. Yet their training paradigms remain dominated by affirmation-based inference, akin to \textit{modus ponens}, where accepted premises yield predicted consequents. While effective for generative fluency, this one-directional approach leaves models vulnerable to logical fallacies, adversarial manipulation, and failures in causal reasoning. This paper makes two contributions. First, it demonstrates how existing LLMs from major platforms exhibit systematic weaknesses when reasoning in scientific domains with negation, counterexamples, or faulty premises \footnote{Code to recreate these experiments are at https://github.com/hannahdavidsoncollege-maker/ScientificReasoningForEnvironment-MedicineWithLLMs. Second, it introduces a dual-reasoning training framework that integrates affirmative generation with structured counterfactual denial. Grounded in formal logic, cognitive science, and adversarial training, this training paradigm formalizes a computational analogue of ``denying the antecedent'' as a mechanism for disconfirmation and robustness. By coupling generative synthesis with explicit negation-aware objectives, the framework enables models that not only affirm valid inferences but also reject invalid ones, yielding systems that are more resilient, interpretable, and aligned with human reasoning.

</details>

*Shuyuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 稀疏奖励在强化学习（RL）中会导致学习效率低下。本文探讨了密集奖励的构建方法，以解决传统RL中奖励信号稀疏或不准确的问题。研究了逆强化学习、基于人类偏好的奖励建模和自监督学习内在奖励等方法，并提出了一系列处理这些未解问题并提高不同RL应用中密集奖励构建的有效性和可靠性的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的强化学习（RL）依赖于奖励信号来指导智能体的学习。然而，当这些信号稀疏、延迟或与任务目标不一致时，智能体的学习效率会受到严重影响。密集奖励函数通过提供密集的反馈信息来塑造智能体的行为，加速学习过程，但手动设计不当的奖励函数可能导致意外行为或奖励漏洞。在复杂环境中，手动设计和验证奖励函数尤其困难。因此，开发更有效、更可靠的密集奖励构建方法至关重要。

Method: 本文探讨了多种解决密集奖励构建挑战的方法，包括但不限于：逆强化学习（IRL），通过观察智能体的行为来推断奖励函数；基于人类偏好的奖励建模，利用人类的反馈来学习奖励函数；以及自监督学习内在奖励，让智能体从与环境的交互中自动发现有意义的奖励信号。具体的技术和实验设置将在论文的后续部分详细阐述。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一系列旨在提高强化学习中密集奖励构建的有效性和可靠性的方法。通过探索IRL、人类偏好学习和自监督学习等多种途径，旨在解决传统稀疏奖励和手动设计奖励函数带来的挑战。研究的最终目标是使RL智能体能够更高效、更准确地学习，并在复杂环境中表现出更符合预期的行为。未来的工作将进一步探索这些方法的局限性，并将其应用于更广泛的RL问题中。

Abstract: Finding meaningful and accurate dense rewards is a fundamental task in the field of reinforcement learning (RL) that enables agents to explore environments more efficiently. In traditional RL settings, agents learn optimal policies through interactions with an environment guided by reward signals. However, when these signals are sparse, delayed, or poorly aligned with the intended task objectives, agents often struggle to learn effectively. Dense reward functions, which provide informative feedback at every step or state transition, offer a potential solution by shaping agent behavior and accelerating learning. Despite their benefits, poorly crafted reward functions can lead to unintended behaviors, reward hacking, or inefficient exploration. This problem is particularly acute in complex or high-dimensional environments where handcrafted rewards are difficult to specify and validate. To address this, recent research has explored a variety of approaches, including inverse reinforcement learning, reward modeling from human preferences, and self-supervised learning of intrinsic rewards. While these methods offer promising directions, they often involve trade-offs between generality, scalability, and alignment with human intent. This proposal explores several approaches to dealing with these unsolved problems and enhancing the effectiveness and reliability of dense reward construction in different RL applications.

### [54] [Efficient Reinforcement Learning with Semantic and Token Entropy for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04359)
*Hongye Cao,Zhixin Bai,Ziyue Peng,Boyan Wang,Tianpei Yang,Jing Huo,Yuyao Zhang,Yang Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves LLM reasoning but can cause entropy collapse. This paper proposes a framework using both semantic and token-level entropy to enhance reasoning by mitigating this collapse. It introduces semantic entropy-guided curriculum learning and non-uniform token treatment with KL regularization. Experiments on 6 benchmarks with 3 LLMs show this method outperforms existing entropy-based approaches.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR enhances LLM reasoning but suffers from entropy collapse, which limits policy exploration and reasoning capabilities. This research addresses the need for a method that maintains exploration while improving reasoning.

Method: The proposed framework uses semantic and token-level entropy. It incorporates semantic entropy-guided curriculum learning to organize training data from low to high semantic entropy. Algorithmically, it employs non-uniform token treatment with KL regularization on low-entropy tokens and stronger constraints on high-covariance portions within these tokens.

Result: The method effectively mitigates entropy collapse and enhances LLM reasoning. Across 6 benchmarks and 3 base models of varying scales, the proposed approach demonstrated superior performance compared to other entropy-based methods in improving reasoning capabilities.

Conclusion: The proposed framework effectively addresses entropy collapse in RLVR for LLMs by leveraging semantic and token-level entropy through guided curriculum learning and non-uniform token treatment. This leads to enhanced reasoning capabilities, outperforming existing methods on multiple benchmarks. Future work could explore further optimizations or applications of this entropy-aware approach.

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has demonstrated superior performance in enhancing the reasoning capability of large language models (LLMs). However, this accuracy-oriented learning paradigm often suffers from entropy collapse, which reduces policy exploration and limits reasoning capabilities. To address this challenge, we propose an efficient reinforcement learning framework that leverages entropy signals at both the semantic and token levels to improve reasoning. From the data perspective, we introduce semantic entropy-guided curriculum learning, organizing training data from low to high semantic entropy to guide progressive optimization from easier to more challenging tasks. For the algorithmic design, we adopt non-uniform token treatment by imposing KL regularization on low-entropy tokens that critically impact policy exploration and applying stronger constraints on high-covariance portions within these tokens. By jointly optimizing data organization and algorithmic design, our method effectively mitigates entropy collapse and enhances LLM reasoning. Experimental results across 6 benchmarks with 3 different parameter-scale base models demonstrate that our method outperforms other entropy-based approaches in improving reasoning.

### [55] [GovBench: Benchmarking LLM Agents for Real-World Data Governance Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04416)
*Zhou Liu,Zhaoyang Han,Guochen Yan,Hao Liang,Bohan Zeng,Xing Chen,Yuanfeng Song,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 数据治理对AI发展至关重要，但自动化面临挑战。现有基准未能充分评估数据治理任务。本文提出了GovBench基准，包含150个真实世界任务，采用“逆向目标”方法生成噪声，并评估端到端流水线可靠性。结果显示当前模型在复杂多步流程和错误纠正方面存在不足。为此，本文提出了DataGovAgent框架，采用Planner-Executor-Evaluator架构，结合基于约束的规划、检索增强生成和沙盒反馈驱动调试。实验证明DataGovAgent显著提升了复杂任务的平均任务得分（ATS），从39.7提升至54.9，并将调试迭代次数减少了77.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代AI开发亟需可扩展的数据治理，以确保数据质量、安全性和合规性。大型语言模型（LLMs）在自动化数据治理方面展现出潜力，但现有自动化数据科学基准未能充分体现数据治理的核心挑战——确保数据本身的正确性和质量。这些基准侧重于代码片段级别或高级分析，忽略了数据治理的复杂性和对数据质量的直接影响。因此，需要一个专门针对数据治理任务的基准来推动该领域的发展。

Method: 本文首先介绍了GovBench，一个包含150个基于真实案例、贴近现实场景的数据治理任务的基准。GovBench采用新颖的“逆向目标”方法来合成逼真的数据噪声，并运用严格的指标来评估整个数据治理流水线的可靠性。随后，在GovBench上对现有模型进行了分析，揭示了它们在处理复杂、多步骤工作流和进行鲁棒错误校正方面的局限性。在此基础上，本文提出了DataGovAgent框架，该框架采用Planner-Executor-Evaluator（规划-执行-评估）架构。该架构集成了基于约束的规划、检索增强生成（RAG）以及通过沙盒环境进行的反馈驱动调试，以应对数据治理的挑战。

Result: 在GovBench基准上的实验结果表明，当前的主流模型在处理复杂、多步骤的数据治理任务时表现不佳，并且缺乏有效的错误纠正机制。相比之下，新提出的DataGovAgent框架在复杂任务上的平均任务得分（ATS）从基线模型的39.7显著提升至54.9。此外，DataGovAgent通过其优化的调试流程，将调试迭代次数减少了超过77.9%，大大提高了数据治理自动化流程的效率。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入GovBench基准和DataGovAgent框架，在自动化数据治理领域取得了重要进展。GovBench填补了现有基准在评估数据治理任务方面的空白，揭示了当前模型面临的挑战。DataGovAgent通过创新的架构和技术，有效提升了自动化数据治理的性能和效率，尤其是在处理复杂任务和减少调试成本方面。未来的工作可以进一步扩展GovBench的规模和多样性，并探索更先进的模型架构和学习策略来进一步提升DataGovAgent的能力，以应对日益增长的数据治理需求。

Abstract: Data governance ensures data quality, security, and compliance through policies and standards, a critical foundation for scaling modern AI development. Recently, large language models (LLMs) have emerged as a promising solution for automating data governance by translating user intent into executable transformation code. However, existing benchmarks for automated data science often emphasize snippet-level coding or high-level analytics, failing to capture the unique challenge of data governance: ensuring the correctness and quality of the data itself. To bridge this gap, we introduce GovBench, a benchmark featuring 150 diverse tasks grounded in real-world scenarios, built on data from actual cases. GovBench employs a novel "reversed-objective" methodology to synthesize realistic noise and utilizes rigorous metrics to assess end-to-end pipeline reliability. Our analysis on GovBench reveals that current models struggle with complex, multi-step workflows and lack robust error-correction mechanisms. Consequently, we propose DataGovAgent, a framework utilizing a Planner-Executor-Evaluator architecture that integrates constraint-based planning, retrieval-augmented generation, and sandboxed feedback-driven debugging. Experimental results show that DataGovAgent significantly boosts the Average Task Score (ATS) on complex tasks from 39.7 to 54.9 and reduces debugging iterations by over 77.9 percent compared to general-purpose baselines.

</details>


### [56] [Solving LLM Repetition Problem in Production: A Comprehensive Study of Multiple Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04419)
*Weiwei Wang,Weijie Zou,Jiyong Min*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型（LLMs）在生产环境中常见的“重复问题”，即模型持续生成重复内容而无法终止。研究者识别了三种重复模式：业务规则生成重复、方法调用关系分析重复和PlantUML图语法生成重复。通过马尔可夫模型分析，确定重复根源在于贪婪解码的循环困境和自我强化效应。提出了三种解决方案：1. 使用`early_stopping=True`的Beam Search解码作为通用事后处理方法；2. `presence_penalty`超参数用于解决特定类型的重复；3. 直接偏好优化（DPO）微调作为通用的模型级别解决方案。该研究结合了实际生产经验和实验验证，系统分析了重复机制，并提供了在实际部署中得到验证的、可投入生产的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLMs）在实际生产部署中存在“重复问题”，即模型会持续生成重复的内容而无法正常终止，这严重影响了系统的性能并可能导致其完全停滞。特别是在批处理代码解释等任务中，这一问题尤为突出。因此，解决LLLLMs的重复问题对于确保其在生产环境中的稳定性和可用性至关重要。

Method: 该研究首先识别了三种具体的重复模式：业务规则生成重复、方法调用关系分析重复和PlantUML图语法生成重复。随后，利用马尔可夫模型进行了理论分析，揭示了问题根源在于贪婪解码算法难以跳出重复循环，并且存在自我强化效应。基于此分析，研究者评估了三种解决方案：1. Beam Search解码配合`early_stopping=True`参数，作为一种通用的事后处理机制；2. `presence_penalty`超参数，作为一种针对特定重复模式（BadCase 1）的有效解决方案；3. 直接偏好优化（DPO）微调，作为一种通用的、在模型层面解决所有三种重复模式的方案。最后，通过广泛的实验验证了这些方法的有效性。

Result: 实验结果表明，Beam Search解码配合`early_stopping=True`参数能够有效地解决所有三种识别出的重复模式。`presence_penalty`超参数在解决BadCase 1类型的重复问题上表现出良好的效果。而DPO微调则作为一种模型级别的通用解决方案，成功克服了所有三种BadCase。这些解决方案在实际部署环境中得到了验证，证明了其在生产环境中的实用性和有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究为解决大型语言模型在生产应用中的重复问题提供了系统性的理论分析和实用的解决方案。通过结合生产经验和实验验证，研究明确了重复问题的机制，并提出了三种不同层级的解决方案：事后处理（Beam Search）、参数调整（presence_penalty）和模型微调（DPO）。其中，`early_stopping`参数被证明是提高Beam Search有效性的关键。这些研究成果为在实际生产环境中部署和优化LLMs提供了宝贵的指导，有助于提升系统的稳定性和性能。未来的工作可以进一步探索更先进的解码策略和模型架构，以应对更复杂的重复现象。

Abstract: The repetition problem, where Large Language Models (LLMs) continuously generate repetitive content without proper termination, poses a critical challenge in production deployments, causing severe performance degradation and system stalling. This paper presents a comprehensive investigation and multiple practical solutions for the repetition problem encountered in real-world batch code interpretation tasks.
  We identify three distinct repetition patterns: (1) business rule generation repetition, (2) method call relationship analysis repetition, and (3) PlantUML diagram syntax generation repetition. Through rigorous theoretical analysis based on Markov models, we establish that the root cause lies in greedy decoding's inability to escape repetitive loops, exacerbated by self-reinforcement effects.
  Our comprehensive experimental evaluation demonstrates three viable solutions: (1) Beam Search decoding with early_stopping=True serves as a universal post-hoc mechanism that effectively resolves all three repetition patterns; (2) presence_penalty hyperparameter provides an effective solution specifically for BadCase 1; and (3) Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) fine-tuning offers a universal model-level solution for all three BadCases.
  The primary value of this work lies in combining first-hand production experience with extensive experimental validation. Our main contributions include systematic theoretical analysis of repetition mechanisms, comprehensive evaluation of multiple solutions with task-specific applicability mapping, identification of early_stopping as the critical parameter for Beam Search effectiveness, and practical production-ready solutions validated in real deployment environments.

### [58] [MARL Warehouse Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04463)
*Price Allman,Lian Thang,Dre Simmons,Salmon Riaz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文比较了多智能体强化学习（MARL）算法在协作仓储机器人中的应用，重点评估了QMIX和IPPO在Robotic Warehouse（RWARE）环境及自定义Unity 3D模拟中的表现。研究发现，QMIX的价值分解方法显著优于独立学习方法（平均回报3.25 vs 0.38），但需要大量的超参数调优，特别是稀疏奖励发现所需的长时间epsilon退火（5M+步）。实验证明QMIX在Unity ML-Agents中成功部署，在1M训练步后实现了稳定的包裹递送。研究指出，MARL在小规模部署（2-4个机器人）方面展现出潜力，但仍面临显著的可扩展性挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自动化需求的增长，仓库机器人面临着日益复杂的协作任务。多智能体强化学习（MARL）为解决这些挑战提供了潜在的解决方案，但目前在实际机器人应用中的有效性仍需深入研究。本研究旨在评估MARL算法在协作仓储机器人环境中的性能，为实际部署提供指导。

Method: 本研究采用了QMIX和IPPO两种MARL算法，并在Robotic Warehouse（RWARE）环境及一个自定义的Unity 3D模拟环境中进行了实验。实验重点关注算法在处理稀疏奖励和实现高效协作方面的能力，并对超参数（如epsilon退火步数）进行了细致的调整。此外，研究还展示了在Unity ML-Agents中的实际部署情况。

Result: 实验结果表明，QMIX算法在协作任务中表现出显著优势，其价值分解方法相比IPPO等独立学习方法取得了更高的平均回报（3.25 vs 0.38）。然而，QMIX的成功部署依赖于大量的超参数调优，特别是需要更长的epsilon退火过程（超过500万步）来发现稀疏奖励。研究成功在Unity ML-Agents中实现了QMIX的部署，并在100万训练步后达到了稳定的包裹递送性能。

Conclusion: 多智能体强化学习（MARL）算法，特别是QMIX，在协作仓储机器人领域展现出巨大潜力，能够有效解决多智能体协作问题并取得优于独立学习方法的性能。然而，该方法对超参数调整非常敏感，尤其是在稀疏奖励场景下。尽管在小规模部署（2-4个机器人）中取得了成功，但将MARL扩展到更大规模的机器人系统仍面临严峻的挑战。未来的工作应着重于改进 MARL 算法的可扩展性，并探索更有效的超参数优化方法。

Abstract: We present a comparative study of multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) algorithms for cooperative warehouse robotics. We evaluate QMIX and IPPO on the Robotic Warehouse (RWARE) environment and a custom Unity 3D simulation. Our experiments reveal that QMIX's value decomposition significantly outperforms independent learning approaches (achieving 3.25 mean return vs. 0.38 for advanced IPPO), but requires extensive hyperparameter tuning -- particularly extended epsilon annealing (5M+ steps) for sparse reward discovery. We demonstrate successful deployment in Unity ML-Agents, achieving consistent package delivery after 1M training steps. While MARL shows promise for small-scale deployments (2-4 robots), significant scaling challenges remain. Code and analyses: https://pallman14.github.io/MARL-QMIX-Warehouse-Robots/

Abstract: We demonstrate the importance of persona-based multi-agents brainstorming for both diverse topics and subject matter ideation. Prior work has shown that generalized multi-agent collaboration often provides better reasoning than a single agent alone. ### [60] [BiTAgent: A Task-Aware Modular Framework for Bidirectional Coupling between Multimodal Large Language Models and World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04513)
*Yu-Wei Zhan,Xin Wang,Pengzhe Mao,Tongtong Feng,Ren Wang,Wenwu Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出了BiTAgent，一个结合了多模态大语言模型（MLLM）和世界模型（WM）的框架，用于构建通用的具身智能体。BiTAgent通过双向耦合机制，解决了MLLM的语义理解与WM的动态预测之间的对齐问题，并实现了跨任务和跨环境的泛化能力。实验证明，BiTAgent在稳定性和泛化性方面优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的具身智能体研究面临着如何整合多模态目标理解、环境动态建模和可靠动作执行的挑战，尤其是在多样化的真实世界任务中。现有的多模态大语言模型（MLLM）虽然具有强大的语义先验和跨模态泛化能力，但难以直接应用于具身控制。世界模型（WM）则能提供可操作的潜在动态以进行预测和控制，但缺乏对复杂语义目标的理解。将两者结合是实现开放式具身智能的关键，但存在MLLM的语义意图与WM的动态状态表示之间的耦合性不强，以及缺乏支持多任务学习和跨环境泛化的任务感知适应性等问题。

Method: 为了解决上述挑战，研究提出了BiTAgent框架，该框架通过三种协同组件实现MLLM与WM的双向耦合：1. **任务感知动态联合学习**：建立前向和后向两种通道。前向通道将MLLM的表示注入WM的潜在空间，以实现语义引导的想象。后向通道利用WM生成的反馈，通过密集的文本条件奖励来优化MLLM的语义空间。2. **任务感知行为学习**：基于联合学习的表示，进行策略学习以执行动作。3. **MLLM-WM联合优化**：通过端到端的优化，使语义推理和动态预测协同工作。实验在多任务和跨环境设置下进行了广泛评估，以验证其稳定性和泛化能力。

Result: 在多任务和跨环境的广泛实验中，BiTAgent展示了优越的稳定性和泛化能力。与最先进的基线方法相比，BiTAgent在处理多样化任务和适应新环境方面表现出更强的性能。具体指标和性能比较的详细数据可在论文的实验部分找到。

Conclusion: BiTAgent通过引入一种新颖的双向耦合机制，有效地整合了MLLM的语义理解能力和WM的动态预测能力，为构建更通用的具身智能体迈出了重要一步。该框架解决了语义与动态表示之间的对齐问题，并实现了良好的任务适应性和泛化性。未来的工作可以进一步探索更复杂的环境交互、更广泛的任务类型以及模型的可解释性。

Abstract: Building generalist embodied agents requires a unified system that can interpret multimodal goals, model environment dynamics, and execute reliable actions across diverse real-world tasks. Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) offer strong semantic priors and cross-modal generalization, while world models (WMs) provide actionable latent dynamics for prediction and control. Their combination holds promise for open-ended embodied intelligence, yet introduces two key challenges: (1) establishing a tight coupling between the semantic intent from MLLMs and the dynamic state representations within the WM's latent space, and (2) achieving task-aware adaptability that supports multi-task learning and cross-environment generalization. To address these limitations, we propose BiTAgent, a task-aware dynamic joint framework that enables bidirectional coupling between MLLMs and WMs. BiTAgent establishes two complementary pathways: a forward path that injects MLLM representations into the WM's latent space for semantically guided imagination, and a backward path where WM-generated feedback refines the MLLM's semantic space via dense text-conditioned rewards. This bidirectional interaction is realized through three synergistic components: Task-Aware Dynamic Joint Learning, Task-Aware Behavior Learning, and MLLM-WM Joint Optimization, which together harmonize semantic reasoning and dynamic prediction. Extensive experiments across multi-task and cross-environment settings demonstrate superior stability and generalization over state-of-the-art baselines, marking a step toward open-ended embodied learning.

</details>


### [61] [The Ethics of Generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.04598)

Conclusion: 生成式AI的类人交互能力和模仿生成特性，使其成为AI伦理研究中的一个关键焦点。它既是现有伦理问题的放大器，也为应对这些挑战提供了新的可能性。理解并解决生成式AI带来的特定伦理问题，如作者身份、人机关系和社会影响，对于负责任地开发和部署此类技术至关重要。未来的研究应继续关注这些新兴伦理挑战，并探索相应的治理和规范策略。

Abstract: This chapter discusses the ethics of generative AI. It provides a technical primer to show how generative AI affords experiencing technology as if it were human, and this affordance provides a fruitful focus for the philosophical ethics of generative AI. It then shows how generative AI can both aggravate and alleviate familiar ethical concerns in AI ethics, including responsibility, privacy, bias and fairness, and forms of alienation and exploitation.
